<li>crimson <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<ol><li>little, few</li>
<li>too little, too few
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1971</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Rozhdestvensky" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Rozhdestvensky">Robert Rozhdestvensky</a> (lyrics), <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arno_Babajanian" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Arno Babajanian">Arno Babajanian</a> (music),  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свадьба.html>сва́дьба</a></span>” | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.karaoke.ru/artists/magomaev-muslim/text/svadba/">[1]</a></sup>, performed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Muslim_Magomayev_(musician)" class="extiw" title="w:Muslim Magomayev (musician)">Muslim Magomayev</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:широкий.html>широ́кой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свадьба.html>сва́дьбе</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́ста</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ло</a></b> / <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>не́ба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ло</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земли́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Širókoj étoj svádʹbe býlo mésta <b>málo</b> / I néba býlo <b>málo</b>, i zemlí.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">For this wide wedding, there was <b>too little</b> space, / And <b>too little</b> sky, and land.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:малограмотный.html>малогра́мотный</a> (23034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mályj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грамотный.html>гра́мотный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grámotnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:малограмотный.html>малогра́мотный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">malográmotnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)малогра́мотнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)малогра́мотней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>semiliterate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> illiterate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">badly versed in an area of knowledge</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:технически.html>техни́чески</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:малограмотный.html>малогра́мотный</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">texníčeski <b>malográmotnyj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">technically <b>illiterate</b>, technologically <b>illiterate</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>completed without sufficient knowledge or without following the rules</li></ol>

***малочисленный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:малочисленный.html>малочи́сленный</a> (27278)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mályj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čisló</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:малочисленный.html>малочи́сленный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maločíslennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>scanty, few, not numerous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:малочисленный.html>малочи́сленные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чаи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maločíslennyje</b> slúčai</i> ― <span class="e-translation">few/isolated cases</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>small
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:малочисленный.html>малочи́сленные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:группа.html>гру́ппы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:население.html>населе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maločíslennyje</b> grúppy naselénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">small population groups</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:малочисленный.html>малочи́сленные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́ды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maločíslennyje</b> naródy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">smaller peoples</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***малый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лый</a> (5075)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">малъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">malŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*malъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)mal-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)mel-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">small</i>.   Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">малий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">malyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mályj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ме́ньше</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:малейший.html>мале́йший</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меньший.html>ме́ньший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>small, little</li>
<li>short</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">short form only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> too small; smaller than necessary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоги́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>малы́</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éti sapogí mne <b>malý</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">These boots are too small for me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>A special short form is found in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>вели́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot <b>mála</b> do velíka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all ages</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from small to big</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Here, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ла</a></b> and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>вели́ка</a></b> are old short genitives.</li>
<li>A special short form is found in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куча.html>ку́ча</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мала́</a></b></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúča <b>malá</b></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pile of people, disorderly heap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small pile</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Here, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мала́</a></b> is an old short feminine attributive adjective.</li>
<li>A special short form is found in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мал</a></b> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мала́</a></b> ме́ньше</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><b>mal</b> <b>malá</b> ménʹše</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one (child, object, etc.) smaller than the next</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small smaller</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Here, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мал</a></b> (masculine) and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>мала́</a></b> (feminine) are old short attributive adjectives.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">малить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">malitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меньший.html>ме́ньший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ménʹšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меньшой.html>меньшо́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">menʹšoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наименьший.html>наиме́ньший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">naiménʹšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ма́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лый</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a/b. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>ме́ньше (поме́ньше), <a href = vnd.unilang:меньший.html>ме́ньший</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:меньший.html>ме́ньшее</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:меньший.html>ме́ньшая</a>).</i>
<a href = vnd.unilang:превосходный.html>Превосхо́дная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:наименьший.html>наиме́ньший</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мал-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.
</p>

<p><b>ма́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лый</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, адъективное <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a/b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мал-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчишеский.html>мальчи́шеский</a> (7516)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мальчи́ш(ка)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">malʹčíš(ka)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-eskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчишеский.html>мальчи́шеский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">malʹčíšeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>boyish, puerile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчишеский.html>мальчи́шеские</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поступок.html>посту́пки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>malʹčíšeskije</b> postúpki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">boyish behaviour</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***малявка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:малявка.html>маля́вка</a> (31110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*maljavъka</i> (compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">маляўка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maljaŭka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span></span> dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">malawka</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:малявка.html>маля́вка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maljavka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*maljava</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ъka</i> whence <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span></span> dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">маля́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maljáva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (also, compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">malavý</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macedonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Macedonian language">Macedonian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk">малав</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">malav</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">malava</i>), further from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*malъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small; little</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ava</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a lang="ine-pro">*(s)mel-</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мамаша.html>мама́ша</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mamáša</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мамаша.html>мама́ши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мамаша.html>мама́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мамаша.html>мама́ш</a></b>)

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мам-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
